        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

#RCA



<span class="line"><!---->#RCA<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





HighlightPseudoStyle calls ComputedStyle-related functions and returns const ComputedStyle*[3].



<span class="line"><!---->HighlightPseudoStyle calls ComputedStyle-related functions and returns const ComputedStyle*[3].<!----></span>



<br>





HighlightPseudoStyle itself wraps const ComputedStyle* and returns a scoped_refptr<const ComputedStyle>[2].



<span class="line"><!---->HighlightPseudoStyle itself wraps const ComputedStyle* and returns a scoped_refptr&lt;const ComputedStyle&gt;[2].<!----></span>



<br>





LayerPaintState calls HighlightPseudoStyle to obtain a scoped_refptr<const ComputedStyle> temporary variable, but uses get()[1] to obtain the original pointer, which leads ComputedStyle get freed and results in UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->LayerPaintState calls HighlightPseudoStyle to obtain a scoped_refptr&lt;const ComputedStyle&gt; temporary variable, but uses get()[1] to obtain the original pointer, which leads ComputedStyle get freed and results in UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>





CSS highlight painting: fix heap-use-after-free and NOTREACHED bugs



<span class="line"><!---->CSS highlight painting: fix heap-use-after-free and NOTREACHED bugs<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The ctor for NGHighlightPainter stores the ComputedStyle for each



<span class="line"><!---->The ctor for NGHighlightPainter stores the ComputedStyle for each<!----></span>



<br>





highlight pseudo in a LayerPaintState field for use by later method



<span class="line"><!---->highlight pseudo in a LayerPaintState field for use by later method<!----></span>



<br>





calls, but it unwraps the scoped_refptr<ComputedStyle> into a raw



<span class="line"><!---->calls, but it unwraps the scoped_refptr&lt;ComputedStyle&gt; into a raw<!----></span>



<br>





pointer first, allowing the values to be freed before use. This patch



<span class="line"><!---->pointer first, allowing the values to be freed before use. This patch<!----></span>



<br>





makes LayerPaintState hold the refcounted pointer itself.



<span class="line"><!---->makes LayerPaintState hold the refcounted pointer itself.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





ForcedForegroundColor and ForcedBackgroundColor lacked cases for the



<span class="line"><!---->ForcedForegroundColor and ForcedBackgroundColor lacked cases for the<!----></span>



<br>





::spelling-error and ::grammar-error pseudos, yielding a NOTREACHED()



<span class="line"><!---->::spelling-error and ::grammar-error pseudos, yielding a NOTREACHED()<!----></span>



<br>





crash when painting those highlights in forced colors mode. This patch



<span class="line"><!---->crash when painting those highlights in forced colors mode. This patch<!----></span>



<br>





adds cases for those pseudos, fixing the crash.



<span class="line"><!---->adds cases for those pseudos, fixing the crash.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Fixed: 1422533



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1422533" title="Heap-use-after-free in blink::NGTextDecorationPainter::UpdateDecorationInfo"><!---->Fixed: 1422533<!----></a>

Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
